```python
def variance(data):
    _type = str(type(data))
    print(_type)
    ft = "<class '{}'>"
    if _type == ft.format("str"):
        data = [float(e) for e in data.split()]
    elif _type == ft.format("list") or _type == ft.format("tuple"):
        pass
    else:
        return tuple()
    n = len(data)
    tilde_x = sum(data)/n
    vatianced = sum([(num-tilde_x)**2 for num in data])/n
    return vatianced

```python
def memovar(data):
    '''
    Return mean,mode,vartiance of the data
    '''
    # Handle the data inputed
    _type = str(type(data))
    ft = "<class '{}'>"
    if _type == ft.format("str"):
        data = [float(e) for e in data.split()]
    elif _type == ft.format("list") or _type == ft.format("tuple"):
        pass
    else:
        return tuple()
    # length
    n = len(data)
    # mean
    tilde_x = sum(data)/n
    # mode
    ifnomode = True
    count_values = []
    for e in set(data):
        count_values.append((e,data.count(e)))
    for index,(e,count) in enumerate(count_values[:-2:1]):
        if count != count_values[index+1][1]:
            ifnomode = False
            break
    count_values = sorted(count_values,key=lambda x:x[1])
    print(count_values)
    mode = []
    if ifnomode == False:
        mode += [e for e,count in count_values if count == count_values[-1][1]]
    else:
        pass
    # vartiance
    vartianced = sum([(num-tilde_x)**2 for num in data])/n
    return (tilde_x,mode,vartianced)

```python
def memovar(data):
    '''
    Return mean,mode,median,vartiance of the data
    '''
    # Handle the data inputed
    _type = str(type(data))
    ft = "<class '{}'>"
    if _type == ft.format("str"):
        data = [float(e) for e in data.split()]
    elif _type == ft.format("list") or _type == ft.format("tuple"):
        pass
    else:
        return tuple()
    # length
    n = len(data)
    # mean
    tilde_x = sum(data)/n
    # mode
    ifnomode = True
    count_values = []
    for e in set(data):
        count_values.append((e,data.count(e)))
    for index,(e,count) in enumerate(count_values[:-2:1]):
        if count != count_values[index+1][1]:
            ifnomode = False
            break
    count_values = sorted(count_values,key=lambda x:x[1])
    print(count_values)
    mode = []
    if ifnomode == False:
        mode += [e for e,count in count_values if count == count_values[-1][1]]
    else:
        pass
    # median
    if n%2 == 0:
        median = (count_values[int((n/2)-1)][0]+count_values[int(n/2)][0])/2
    elif n%2 == 1:
        median = count_values[int(((n+1)/2)-1)][0]
    # vartiance
    vartianced = sum([(num-tilde_x)**2 for num in data])/n
    return (tilde_x,mode,median,vartianced)

```python
def mmmrva(data):
    '''
    Return mean,range,mode,median,vartiance of the data
    '''
    class Result:
        def __init__(self,mean,range_,mode,median,vartiance):
            self.mean = mean
            self.range = range_
            self.mode = mode
            self.median = median
            self.vartiance = self.var = vartiance
        def show(self):
            print("mean:{}\nrange:{}\nmode:{}\nmedian:{}\nvartiance:{}".format(self.mean,self.range,self.mode,self.median,self.var))
    # Handle the data inputed
    _type = str(type(data))
    ft = "<class '{}'>"
    if _type == ft.format("str"):
        data = sorted([float(e) for e in data.split()])
    elif _type == ft.format("list") or _type == ft.format("tuple"):
        data = sorted([float(e) for e in data])
    else:
        return tuple()
    # length
    n = len(data)
    # mean
    tilde_x = sum(data)/n
    # range
    range_ = data[-1]-data[0]
    # mode
    count_values = sorted([(e,data.count(e)) for e in set(data)],key=lambda x:x[1])
    if (count_values[-1][1]-count_values[0][1]) == 0:ifnomode = True
    else:ifnomode = False
    mode = []
    if ifnomode == False:
        mode += [e for e,count in count_values if count == count_values[-1][1]]
    # median
    if n%2 == 0:
        median = (data[int(n/2)-1]+data[int(n/2)])/2
    elif n%2 == 1:
        median = data[int(((n+1)/2)-1)]
    # vartiance
    vartianced = sum([(num-tilde_x)**2 for num in data])/n
    return Result(tilde_x,range_,mode,median,vartianced)

大写：陆
拼音：liù
进位制：六进制
因数分解：2×3
因数：1、2、3、6（为2和3的最小公倍数）
罗马数字：VI
二进制：110
八进制：6
十进制：6
十六进制：6
3！=3×2×1=6
Γ(4)=6
第三个三角数。

并联
$W=W_1+W_2$
$W=UI_1t+UI_2t$
$W=I_1R_1I_1t+I_2R_2I_2t$
$W=I_1^{2}R_1t+I_2^{2}R_2t$
$W=UI_1t+UI_2t$
$W=U(I_1+I_2)t$

串联
$I^{2}=I\frac{U}{R1+R2}$
$I^{2}=(\frac{U}{R1+R2})^{2}$
$I^{2}(R_1+R_2)t=(\frac{U}{R_1+R_2})^{2}(R_1+R_2)t$
$W=U_总It$

```python
def mmmrva(data=None):
    '''
    Return mean,range,mode,median,vartiance of the data
    Args:
        data:list or str or Nonetype -> the data
    '''
    class Result:
        def __init__(self,mean,range_,mode,median,vartiance):
            self.mean = mean
            self.range = range_
            self.mode = mode
            self.median = median
            self.vartiance = self.var = vartiance
        def show(self):
            print("mean:{}\nrange:{}\nmode:{}\nmedian:{}\nvartiance:{}".format(
                self.mean,self.range,self.mode,self.median,self.var))
    if data==None:data = input()
    # Handle the data inputed
    _type = str(type(data))
    ft = "<class '{}'>"
    if _type == ft.format("str"):
        data = sorted([float(e) for e in data.split()])
    elif _type == ft.format("list") or _type == ft.format("tuple"):
        data = sorted([float(e) for e in data])
    else:
        return tuple()
    # length
    n = len(data)
    # mean
    tilde_x = sum(data)/n
    # range
    range_ = data[-1]-data[0]
    # mode
    count_values = sorted([(e,data.count(e)) for e in set(data)],key=lambda x:x[1])
    if (count_values[-1][1]-count_values[0][1]) == 0:ifnomode = True
    else:ifnomode = False
    mode = []
    if ifnomode == False:
        mode += [e for e,count in count_values if count == count_values[-1][1]]
    # median
    if n%2 == 0:
        median = (data[int(n/2)-1]+data[int(n/2)])/2
    elif n%2 == 1:
        median = data[int(((n+1)/2)-1)]
    # vartiance
    vartianced = sum([(num-tilde_x)**2 for num in data])/n
    result = Result(tilde_x,range_,mode,median,vartianced)
    result.show()
    return result

static int Fib(int n)
        {
            int[] a = new int[n];
            a[0] = 1;
            if (n > 1)
            {
                a[1] = 1;
            }
            for (int i = 2; i < a.Length; i++)
            {
                a[i] = a[i - 1] + a[i - 2];
            }
            return a[n - 1];
        }
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            int n = int.Parse(Console.ReadLine());
            for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++)
            {
                Console.WriteLine(Fib(i));
            }
        }
